 <script>
  $(document).on('click', '.coef-change__button_edit', function () {
        var $this = $(this);
        $this.add($(this).siblings('.coef-value'))
        $this.parent().hide().siblings('.coef-change-item').addClass('active');
    }).on('click', '.coef-change__button_ok', function () {
        var $this = $(this);
        $this.parent().siblings('.coef-value, .coef-change-box').show();
        $this.parent().removeClass('active');
        getCuponUpdate();
    }).on('keypress', '.js-focus-coeff', function (event) {
        var $this = $(this);
        if (event.which === 13) {
            $this.parent().siblings('.coef-value, .coef-change-box').show();
            $this.parent().removeClass('active');
            getCuponUpdate();
        }
    }).on('click', '.coef-change__button_close', function () {
        var $this = $(this);
        $this.parent().siblings('.coef-value, .coef-change-box').show();
        $this.parent().siblings('.coef-change-item__input').val('');
        $this.parent().removeClass('active');
    });
 </script>
